[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-irc.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected a write [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes beyond its boundary. This occurs during the processing of IRC NAMES command [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowed by additional data.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m45[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a multi-byte-write-heap-buffer-overflow. The overflow occurs during a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory copy operation that attempts to write beyond the bounds of an allocated heap[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location of the overflow:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x5060001c64f3[0m[39m`, which is exactly at the end of a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m-byte region allocated at `[0m[1;36m0x5060001c64c0[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The write operation attempts to copy [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes into this [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This results in writing [0m[1;36m81[0m[39m bytes beyond the allocated region[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Stack Analysis:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The fuzzer invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` which triggers [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Overflow**: The overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m563[0m[39m in `dissect_irc_names` during a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_memcpy` operation, which internally calls `memcpy`[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of Code Snippets and Evaluation Report[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause Identified**: Three IRC dissector functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_irc_names`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_irc_join`, `dissect_irc_part`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m contain a critical buffer overflow when [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing comma-separated channel names. They incorrectly use the total remaining [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer length instead of calculating the length up to the comma delimiter.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer Allocation Pattern**: All vulnerable functions allocate a fixed [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CHANNELLEN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` where `[0m[33mCHANNELLEN[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m50[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to hold channel names with null [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtermination.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Symptom Location**: The overflow occurs specifically when `end_offset != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcomma found[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where the code copies `length` bytes instead of `end_offset - [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart_offset` bytes into the [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Correct Reference**: The `dissect_irc_list` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m613[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct implementation pattern that should be followed.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Trigger Condition**: The vulnerability is triggered by comma-separated channel[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames where the first channel name is longer than [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m characters, causing the entire[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremaining buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes in the fuzzer test case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to be copied into the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must address **[0m[1;36m5[0m[39m specific lines** across **[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m functions** in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`epan/dissectors/packet-irc.c`:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Function [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: `dissect_irc_names` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m563[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current buggy code:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend_offset-start_offset < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: When a comma is found [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`end_offset != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the copy length should [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe the distance from `start_offset` to the comma [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`end_offset - start_offset`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe entire remaining buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The ternary operator ensures the copy [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoesn't exceed `CHANNELLEN` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m50[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Function [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: `dissect_irc_join` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m370[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m373[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line [0m[1;36m370[0m[39m - Current buggy code:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? length : [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend_offset-start_offset < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line [0m[1;36m373[0m[39m - Current buggy code:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_irc_request_command_join_channel, tvb, start_offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_irc_request_command_join_channel, tvb, start_offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend_offset-start_offset, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: Similar to `dissect_irc_names`, both the `tvb_memcpy` length [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter and the `proto_tree_add_item` length parameter must use `end_offset - [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart_offset` instead of `length` when processing comma-separated channels. Line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m370[0m[39m has the additional bug of comparing the wrong value in the ternary operator.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Function [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: `dissect_irc_part` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m438[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m441[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line [0m[1;36m438[0m[39m - Current buggy code:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? length : [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend_offset-start_offset < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line [0m[1;36m441[0m[39m - Current buggy code:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_irc_request_command_join_channel, tvb, start_offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_irc_request_command_join_channel, tvb, start_offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend_offset-start_offset, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: Identical issue to `dissect_irc_join`. Both the copy length and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisplay length must be corrected to use the calculated distance to the comma [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdelimiter.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is The Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: The fix only modifies the incorrect length calculations [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout changing the overall logic, data structures, or function signatures. This [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimizes the risk of introducing new bugs or breaking existing functionality.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Pattern**: The fix applies the already-correct pattern from [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_irc_list` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m613[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to the three vulnerable functions, ensuring [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency across the codebase.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves All Paths**: The fix only affects the comma-separated channel [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing path. The [0m[32m"no comma found"[0m[39m path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`end_offset == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas it's already correct in all functions.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Backward Compatibility**: The protocol tree structure, display [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput, and parsing behavior remain identical - only the memory safety issue is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: The fix doesn't modify:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer allocation strategy [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstill uses `[0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCHANNELLEN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory management [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmalloc/free pattern unchanged[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Null termination approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemset still zeroes buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - API signatures or calling conventions[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test expectations or protocol compliance[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses The Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Buffer Overflow**: By correctly calculating the copy length as [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`end_offset - start_offset` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbounded by `CHANNELLEN`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the fix ensures that only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bytes up to the comma delimiter are copied, preventing writes beyond the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Handles Edge Cases**:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Empty channels** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`#a,,#b`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: When `end_offset == start_offset`, the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculation yields [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, which is safe[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Long channels** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m50[0m[39m chars[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The ternary operator truncates to `CHANNELLEN`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining RFC compliance[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Single channels**: Uses the already-correct [0m[32m"no comma"[0m[39m path[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Trailing commas**: Handled correctly by the while loop condition[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fixes Display Length Bug**: In `dissect_irc_join` and `dissect_irc_part`, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item` calls also used the wrong length, which could cause incorrect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol tree display. The fix corrects this as well.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Channel Name Truncation**: Channels longer than [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m characters will be [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated in the `proto_item_append_text` output.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is actually correct behavior per IRC RFC specifications, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich limit channel names to [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m characters. The truncation was already intended [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msee `CHANNELLEN` constant[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Display Differences**: Users might notice slightly different text in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol tree summary for very long channel names.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is a cosmetic change only. The full channel name is still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly displayed in the detailed tree items via `proto_tree_add_item`, which [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses the tvbuff directly.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Regression Risk**: The fix cannot break existing correct behavior because:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The [0m[32m"no comma"[0m[39m path remains untouched [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready correct[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The length calculation for comma-separated names was objectively wrong before[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix aligns with the correct implementation in `dissect_irc_list`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_irc_list` function at line [0m[1;36m613[0m[39m already implements this exact pattern [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend_offset-start_offset < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis proves the fix is compatible with the codebase architecture and has been used [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessfully in production code.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
